----------
TUTORIAL
----------
「<color\=#ffd145>{{B}}</color>」是在<color\=#ffd145>{{A}}</color>出现的神秘高塔，\n需<color\=#ffd145>组建小队</color>前往调查。\n每次进入时，都会生成全新地图，\n让每一场冒险都充满未知的挑战。=[<color\=#ffd145>{{B}}</color>] is a mysterious tower that appears in the <color\=#ffd145>{{A}}</color>,\n<color\=#ffd145>set up a team</color> to investigate.\nA new map is generated on each exploration.
由于{{A}}充满种种疑团，\n在此处您<color\=#ffd145>无法发挥正常实力</color>，\n必须在探索中击败怪物才能<color\=#ffd145>重新提升等级</color>。=You <color\=#ffd145>cannot exert normal strength</color> here,\nneed to defeat foes during exploration to <color\=#ffd145>re-level up</color>.
探索小队的角色阵容也<color\=#ffd145>受到限制</color>，\n在后续游玩时需要收集「<color\=#ffd145>心灵碎片</color>」来逐步<color\=#ffd145>解锁角色</color>。=Characters for exploration team are also <color\=#ffd145>eestricted</color>,\nneed to collect [<color\=#ffd145>Heart Fragments</color>] to gradually<color\=#ffd145>unlock characters</color>.
{{A}}的挑战会<color\=#ffd145>非常困难</color>，\n请努力以攀爬到更高层为目标去挑战吧。={{A}} is <color\=#ffd145>very difficult</color>,\nplease strive to climb to higher floors.
开始「<color\=#ff3b37>{{A}}挑战</color>」=Start [<color\=#ff3b37>{{A}} Challenge</color>]
潜入{{A}}=Infiltrate {{A}}
{{A}}·随行队伍={{A}}·Companion Team
r:"^探索{{A}}，需要确定「<color\=#FFD145>随行队伍</color>」，\n包含<color\=#FFD145>(\d+)名主战</color>角色和<color\=#FFD145>(\d+)名辅助</color>角色。\n这些角色<color\=#FFD145>不在初始队伍</color>中，会在探索中逐步加入。$"="To explore {{A}}, you need a [<color\=#FFD145>Team</color>],\nIncluding <color\=#FFD145>$1 active</color> and <color\=#FFD145>$2 assist</color> characters.\nThese characters <color\=#FFD145>do not start in the initial team</color>, and will gradually join in exploration."
开始预设「<color\=#ff3b37>随行角色</color>」=Select [<color\=#ff3b37>Companion Character</color>]
{{A}}·随行角色={{A}}·Companion Character
<color\=#FFD145>无论是否拥有</color>角色，\n均可以选择其作为「<color\=#FFD145>随行角色</color>」加入到探索中。\n更多角色需要收集「<color\=#FFD145>心灵碎片</color>」解锁。=<color\=#FFD145>Whether you own them or not</color>,\nyou can still select them as [<color\=#FFD145>companion character</color>] for exploration.\nUnlock more characters with [<color\=#FFD145>Heart Fragments</color>].
也可以「<color\=#ff3b37>快捷编队</color>」=Can [<color\=#ff3b37>Quick Select</color>]
「<color\=#ff3b37>确认选择</color>」立即开始探索=[<color\=#ff3b37>Confirm</color>] to start exploration
{{A}}·洗牌时间={{A}}·Shuffle Time
在{{A}}开始时，将触发「<color\=#FFD145>洗牌时间</color>」：\n将可能性具象化为数种拥有不同效果的卡牌，\n您可从中<color\=#FFD145>选择1张</color>。=At the start of {{A}}, trigger [<color\=#FFD145>Shuffle Time</color>]: You can <color\=#FFD145>choose 1</color> card.
洗牌时间·角色卡牌=Shuffle Time·Character Card
<color\=#FFD145>角色卡首次选择</color>，可加入阵容并可调配上阵。\n角色<color\=#FFD145>再次选择</color>将提升1次意识，至到6意识。\n<color\=#FFD145>S.E.E.S.成员</color>在提升到6意识后，\n再次选择还会觉醒「<color\=#FFD145>超越意识</color>」获得新的能力。=Add character to team after <color\=#FFD145>first choice</color>.\nIncrease Awareness by 1 when <color\=#FFD145>choosing them again</color>, up to Awareness 6.\n<color\=#FFD145>S.E.E.S. Members</color> will awaken <color\=#FFD145>Beyond Awareness</color> when choosing them again after Awareness 6.
洗牌时间·小阿尔卡那卡=Shuffle Time·Minor Arcana
「<color\=#FFD145>权杖</color>」提供暂时的的各种增益。\n「<color\=#FFD145>圣杯</color>」提供永久的探索类增益。\n「<color\=#FFD145>宝剑</color>」提供永久的战斗类增益。\n「<color\=#FFD145>钱币</color>」提供一次性的奖励道具。=[<color\=#FFD145>Wands</color>] provides temporary buffs.\n[<color\=#FFD145>Cups</color>] provides permanent exploration buffs.\n[<color\=#FFD145>Swords</color>] provides permanent combat buffs.\n[<color\=#FFD145>Coins</color>] provide one-time reward items.
洗牌时间·大阿尔卡那卡=Shuffle Time·Major Arcana
偶尔还会出现「<color\=#FFD145>大阿尔卡那卡牌</color>」，\n选择可以获得各类强力的增益效果，\n且获得数量没有限制。=Occasionally, there will be [<color\=#FFD145>Major Arcana Cards</color>], they provide strong buffs, and have no obtain limit.
查看探索「<color\=#ff3b37>状态</color>」=View [<color\=#ff3b37>Condition</color>]
{{A}}·探索等级={{A}}·Exploration Level
在战斗中可获得经验值提升「<color\=#FFD145>探索等级</color>」，\n探索等级将决定：全队<color\=#FFD145>角色</color>等级、<color\=#FFD145>武器</color>等级、<color\=#FFD145>技能</color>等级，以及{{B}}的<color\=#FFD145>{{A}}</color>等级。=Gain <color\=#FFD145>Exploration Level</color> in combat.\nExploration level will determine: All <color\=#FFD145>character</color> level, <color\=#FFD145>weapon</color> level, <color\=#FFD145>skill</color> level, and Wonder <color\=#FFD145>{{A}}</color> level.
{{A}}·意志力={{A}}·Will
战斗后将削减「<color\=#FFD145>意志力</color>」，\n请时刻注意「意志力」的变化，尽量保持<color\=#FFD145>0点</color>以上，\n避免各类严重的<color\=#FFD145>负面效果</color>。=Decrease [<color\=#FFD145>Will</color>] after battle, try to keep [Will] above <color\=#FFD145>0</color> to avoid serious <color\=#FFD145>negative effects</color>.
{{A}}·收获={{A}}·Rewards
收获的奖励将暂时放在「<color\=#FFD145>收获</color>」背包。\n在<color\=#FFD145>探索结束</color>时（无论成功或失败），\n奖励可被带出{{A}}，用于能力的提升。=All rewards are temporarily stored in the <color\=#FFD145>Rewards</color> bag.\nWhen <color\=#FFD145>exploration ends</color> (victory or defeat), rewards can be taken out of {{A}} and used to improve abilities.
因此挑战{{A}}并<color\=#FFD145>不需要以通关为目的</color>，\n能力提升后再来挑战或许会更轻松。=So there is <color\=#FFD145>no need to see victory as the goal</color> in {{A}},\nchallenges may be easier after improving your abilities.
{{A}}·游荡阴影={{A}}·Roaming Shadow
{{A}}中游荡著各种危险的<color\=#FFD145>阴影</color>。\n消灭它们，可以获得<color\=#FFD145>心灵碎片</color>以及<color\=#FFD145>时钟的齿轮</color>。\n战斗胜利后，会进入「<color\=#FFD145>洗牌时间</color>」。={{A}} has many <color\=#FFD145>Roaming Shadows</color>.\nDefeat them to gain <color\=#FFD145>Heart Fragments</color> and <color\=#FFD145>Clock Gears</color>.\nEnter [<color\=#FFD145>Shuffle Time</color>] after battle.
每场战斗后，会<color\=#FFD145>恢复全部HP和SP</color>，\n死亡的角色也会复活。=After each battle, <color\=#FFD145>fully restore all HP and SP</color>,\nrevive all dead characters.
{{A}}·宝箱={{A}}·Treasure Chest
探索{{A}}时会找到<color\=#FFD145>宝箱</color>，\n可以获得各类珍贵资源，有助于{{A}}的攻略。\n请积极地尝试去寻找吧。=Can find <color\=#FFD145>Treasure Chest</color> when exploring {{A}},\nwhich give various valuable resources, please look for them.
宝箱分为不同种类，\n<color\=#FFD145>低级宝箱</color>：随机获得时钟的齿轮、古老的银币\n<color\=#FFD145>中级宝箱</color>：可以获得拂晓的碎片\n<color\=#FFD145>高级宝箱</color>：获得古老的金币、梦境碎片以及心灵碎片=Treasure chests are divided into different types, \n<color\=#FFD145>Low-level Treasure Chest</color>: Randomly obtain Clock Gears and Ancient Silver Coins\n<color\=#FFD145>Medium Treasure Chest</color>: Obtain Dawn Fragments\n<color\=#FFD145>High-level Treasure Chest</color>: Obtain Ancient Gold Coinss, Dream Fragments, and Heart Fragments
{{A}}·迷雾={{A}}·Fog
{{A}}·红色迷雾={{A}}·Red Fog
在{{A}}中会遇到「<color\=#FFD145>红色迷雾</color>」，\n需要<color\=#FFD145>击败</color>强力阴影的守卫后才能通行。=You will encounter [<color\=#FFD145>Red Fog</color>] in {{A}},\nneed to <color\=#FFD145>defeat</color> the powerful Shadow to pass.
{{A}}·橙色迷雾={{A}}·Orange Fog
「<color\=#FFD145>橙色迷雾</color>」虽然没有强力阴影镇守，\n但需要消耗一定<color\=#FFD145>意志力</color>才能通过。=Although [<color\=#FFD145>Orange Fog</color>] is not guarded, you need to spend <color\=#FFD145>Will</color> to pass.
{{A}}·楼梯={{A}}·Stairs
找到每一层的楼梯，才能进入更高的<color\=#FFD145>楼层</color>。\n请积极地在楼层中寻找。\n一旦决定进入下一层就<color\=#FFD145>无法回头</color>了。=You need to find the stairs to reach higher <color\=#FFD145>floors</color>.\nOnce you decide to enter the next floor, there is <color\=#FFD145>no turning back</color>.
{{A}}·瞬杀={{A}}·Insta-kill
探索时遇到的阴影，\n如果由<color\=#FFD145>红色光焰</color>缠绕，接触后将进入战斗。 \n当「瞬杀能力」强化到一定程度时，阴影的红色光焰会消失，此时攻击将可以<color\=#FFD145>瞬杀阴影</color>。=You can insta-kill Shadows without a <color\=#FFD145>red glow</color>.
{{A}}·瞬杀能力={{A}}·Insta-kill Ability
「瞬杀能力」由<color\=#FFD145>探索等级</color>、上阵角色的<color\=#FFD145>总意识数</color>、全部<color\=#FFD145>增益效果</color>等因素决定。=[Insta-kill Ability] is based on <color\=#FFD145>Exploration Level</color>, <color\=#FFD145>total number of Awareness</color> on active characters, all <color\=#FFD145>buff effects</color> and other factors.
{{A}}·稀有阴影={{A}} Rare Shadow
稀有阴影=Rare Shadow
在探索{{A}}时，偶尔能遇到「<color\=#FFD145>稀有阴影</color>」，\n将其打倒可获得更丰厚的奖励，包括：<color\=#FFD145>古老的银币</color>、<color\=#FFD145>古老的金币</color>、<color\=#FFD145>拂晓的碎片</color>以及大量<color\=#FFD145>时钟的齿轮</color>。=When exploring {{A}}, you can occasionally encounter [<color\=#FFD145>Rare Shadow</color>],\ndefeat them for a bigger reward, including: <color\=#FFD145>Ancient Silver Coins</color>, <color\=#FFD145>Ancient Gold Coins</color>, <color\=#FFD145>Dawn Fragments</color> and many <color\=#FFD145>Clock Gears</color>.
{{A}}·失踪者={{A}}·Missing Person
在{{A}}内，\n有时会遇到误入的「<color\=#FFD145>失踪者</color>」以及认知之猫。=In {{A}},\nsometimes you will encounter [<color\=#FFD145>missing person</color>] and cognitive cat.
与他们对话，可以选择不同的选项来得到不同的结果。\n之后，会将失踪者<color\=#FFD145>自动带离</color>{{A}}。=Talk to them and choose different options to get different results. \nAfter that, the missing person <color\=#FFD145> will automatically leave</color> {{A}}.
{{A}}·大时钟={{A}}·Grand Clock
在{{A}}内可以找到「<color\=#FFD145>大时钟</color>」，\n在「大时钟」处可以消耗「<color\=#FFD145>时钟的齿轮</color>」，\n获得各类具象化的卡牌。=You can find [<color\=#FFD145>Grand Clock</color>] in {{A}},\ncan spend [<color\=#FFD145>Clock Gears</color>] to obtain various cards at [Grand Clock].
{{A}}·时钟={{A}}·Clock
在{{A}}内还能找到「<color\=#FFD145>时钟</color>」，\n消耗「<color\=#FFD145>拂晓的碎片</color>」启动时钟后，\n可以选择<color\=#FFD145>回复意志力</color>或<color\=#FFD145>定向提升角色意识</color>。=You can also find [<color\=#FFD145>Clock</color>] in {{A}},\nafter consuming [<color\=#FFD145>Dawn Fragments</color>], can choose to <color\=#FFD145>restore WIll</color> or <color\=#FFD145>increase character's Awareness</color>.
{{A}}·交错之影={{A}}·Tangled Shadow
可以感知到<color\=#FFD145>下一个</color>将遇到的「<color\=#FFD145>交错之影</color>」情报，\n在挑战前最好根据其特征选定阵容。=Can sense the intel on the <color\=#FFD145>next</color> [<color\=#FFD145>Tangled Shadow</color>], best to parpare your team.
只有战胜强力的「<color\=#FFD145>交错之影</color>」才能进一步前进，\n并获得大量<color\=#FFD145>心灵碎片</color>、<color\=#FFD145>梦境碎片</color>以及<color\=#FFD145>时钟的齿轮</color>。=Can only continue by defeating [<color\=#FFD145>Tangled Shadow</color>], then gain many <color\=#FFD145>Heart Fragments</color>, <color\=#FFD145>Dream Fragments</color> and <color\=#FFD145>Clock Gears</color>.
查看「<color\=#ff3b37>BOSS详情</color>」=View [<color\=#ff3b37>Boss details</color>]
查看「<color\=#ff3b37>真宵堂</color>」=View [<color\=#ff3b37>Mayoido Antiques</color>]
解锁<color\=#ff3b37>收藏品</color>，\n需要消耗「<color\=#ff3b37>古老的金币</color>」=Unlock <color\=#ff3b37>Antique</color>,\nneed to spend [<color\=#ff3b37>Ancient Gold Coins</color>]
解锁<color\=#ff3b37>古董品</color>，\n需要消耗「<color\=#ff3b37>古老的金币</color>」=Unlock <color\=#ff3b37>Antique</color>,\nneed to spend [<color\=#ff3b37>Ancient Gold Coins</color>]

装备<color\=#ff3b37>古董品</color>，\n为探索带来强力增益。=Equip <color\=#ff3b37>Antique</color> to bring powerful buffs to exploration.

{{A}}·永夜之塔={{A}}·Tower of Eternal Night
<color\=#FFD145>全新模式</color>「{{A}}·永夜之塔」现已开放。\n请努力以攀爬到更高层为目标去挑战吧。=<color\=#FFD145>New mode</color>[{{A}}·Tower of Eternal Night] is now available. Please try your best to climb to the higher floor.
{{A}}·核心古董品={{A}}·Core Antique
挑战「{{A}}·永夜之塔」前，需要确定本局的<color\=#FFD145>构筑策略</color>。\n核心古董品会在探索中根据「<color\=#FFD145>探索等级</color>」不断提升，发挥更大的效果。=Before challenging [{{A}}·Tower of Eternal Night], you need to select a <color\=#FFD145>Core Antique</color>.\nCore antique will upgrade during exploration based on [<color\=#FFD145>Exploration Level</color>].
{{A}}·月下羁绊={{A}}·Moonlit Bond
「月下羁绊」可以用来解锁或升级羁绊节点，为「<color\=#ff3b37>全队成员</color>」探索带来基础增益、获取探索技能，使探索更加自如。=[Moonlit Bond] can provide basic buffs and exploration skills to [<color\=#ff3b37>party</color>].

可疑的小哥=Suspicious Man
哟，小帅哥！\n要不要来我店里坐坐？=Yo, handsome!\nDo you want to come to my shop?
我最近刚开了家店，\n结果一个客人也没有，可愁死我了……=I just opened a shop recently and I have not had a single customer, it's killing me...
如果经营不善，就得倒闭关门了不是吗？\n所以我只好出来拼命拉客了。=If I don't do well, I'll have to close down. That's why I have to come out and try my best to get customers.
也不知怎么地就溜达到这鬼地方来了，\n不过我们俩能在这儿碰上，也算是缘分！=I don't know how I got here, but it must be fate that we've met!
怎么样呀小帅哥？就当被我骗一回，\n来我店里瞧瞧呗？=How about it, handsome? Why don't you come to my shop as if you've been tricked by me?
